Rajshahi oncholer biyete thake pithar joyjoykar.
Eisob protisthanguloke ekti notun o osthayi talikate jukto korar prokriya chalu ache, talikatir naam "Purbe Datobbo songstha hishabe porichito chilo je protisthangulo".
